Our free &l;a href=\&q;https://www.udacity.com/course/ud282\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;Java Programming Basics course&l;/a&g; is a good place to start. &l;/p&g; &l;h3&g;Technical Skills and Requirements&l;/h3&g; &l;p&g;Sample code in our courses is shared on GitHub. You must have a GitHub handle and know how to share code on GitHub prior to enrolling. If you don&a;#39;t have Android Studio installed, see our mini-course on &l;a href=\&q;https://www.udacity.com/course/how-to-install-android-studio--ud808\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;How to Install Android Studio&l;/a&g; for instructions.&l;/p&g; &l;h3&g;Dedication and Mindset&l;/h3&g; &l;p&g;In addition to 1-2 years of prior programming experience and intermediate technical skills, students are expected to demonstrate the following characteristics:&l;/p&g; &l;ul&g; &l;li&g;&l;strong&g;Resourcefulness&l;/strong&g;: Ability to search for and find solutions in documentation, backed by the belief that all problems in code are discoverable;&l;/li&g; &l;li&g;&l;strong&g;Grit&l;/strong&g;: Ability to work through challenges and persevere when code breaks and tests fail.&l;/li&g; &l;li&g;&l;strong&g;Growth Mindset&l;/strong&g;: Belief that intelligence is NOT a fixed entity, and can be boosted by hard work in the process of learning and practice.&l;/li&g; &l;/ul&g;&q;,&q;seo_keywords&q;:&q;&q;,&q;selling_points&q;:{&q;images_url&q;:[],&q;selling_keys&q;:[]},&q;short_summary&q;:&q;Start your career as an Android developer.
